index_of_coincidence(text: str) ->/ float: s = _letters_only(text) N = len(s) if N < class="number">2: return class="number">0.0 counts = Counter(s) num = sum(c*(c-class="number">1) for c in counts.values()) den = N*(N-class="number">1) return num/den if den else class="number">0.0 def friedman_estimate_keylen(text: str) ->/ float: class="string">""class="string">"Classic Friedman estimate for Vigenère key length (float)."class="string">"" s = _letters_only(text) N = len(s) if N < class="number">2: return class="number">1.0 IC = index_of_coincidence(s) class=class="string">"comment"># Using standard constants for English K0 = class="number">0.0385 K1 = class="number">0.065 if IC <= class="number">0: return class="number">1.0 num = (K1 - K0) * N den column lengths (last row may be short) short = (w*rows - n) col_len = [rows]*(w-short) + [rows-class="number">1]*short class=class="string">"comment"># order of columns (if permutation not given, use numeric ascending) if keyperm is None: order = list(range(w)) else: order = list(keyperm) if len(order)!=w: order = list(range(w)) class=class="string">"comment"># slice ct into columns by order cols = [None]*w idx=class="number">0 for k in order: L = col_len[k] cols[k] = c[idx:idx+L] idx += L class=class="string">"comment"># read row-wise out=[] for r in range(rows): for k in range(w): if r < len(cols[k]): out.append(cols[k][r]) return class="string">"".join(out) class=class="string">"comment"># ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- class=class="string">"comment"># Key length + key letter guessers (Vigenère family) class=class="string">"comment"># ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- def _chi2_for_shift(coset: str, shift: int) ->/ float: class=class="string">"comment"># Shift coset backwards (decipher) then chi-squared pt = class="string">"".join(_deshift_char(c, shift) for c in coset) class=class="string">"comment"># chi-squared vs English freq = Counter(pt) N = len(pt) or class="number">1 expected = { class="string">'E': class="number">12.702, class="string">'T': class="number">9.056, class="string">'A': class="number">8.167, class="string">'O': class="number">7.507, class="string">'I': class="number">6.966, class="string">'N': class="number">6.749, class="string">'S': class="number">6.327, class="string">'H': class="number">6.094, class="string">'R': class="number">5.987, class="string">'D': class="number">4.253, class="string">'L': class="number">4.025, class="string">'C': class="number">2.782, class="string">'U': class="number">2.758, class="string">'M': class="number">2.406, class="string">'W': class="number">2.360, class="string">'F': class="number">2.228, class="string">'G': class="number">2.015, class="string">'Y': class="number">1.974, class="string">'P': class="number">1.929, class="string">'B': class="number">1.492, class="string">'V': class="number">0.978, class="string">'K': class="number">0.772, class="string">'J': class="number">0.153, class="string">'X': class="number">0.150, class="string">'Q': class="number">0.095, class="string">'Z': class="number">0.074 } chi = class="number">0.0 for ch in ALPHA: o = freq.get(ch,class="number">0) * class="number">100.0 / N e = expected[ch] if e >/ class="number">0: diff = o - e chi += (diff*diff)/e return chi def guess_vigenere_key_by_len(ct: str, m: int, top_k: int = class="number">3) ->/ list[str]: s = _clean_alpha(ct) cosets = split_cosets(s, m) class=class="string">"comment"># best shift per coset (min chi2) shifts = [] for cos in cosets: if not cos: shifts.append(class="number">0); continue best = min(range(class="number">26), key=lambda sh: _chi2_for_shift(cos, sh)) shifts.append(best) class=class="string">"comment"># produce a few alternates by allowing each coset to consider 2nd-best class=class="string">"comment"># compute per-coset ranked shifts ranked = [] for cos in cosets: rnk = sorted(range(class="number">26), key=lambda sh: _chi2_for_shift(cos, sh))[:class="number">2] ranked.append(rnk) keys = set() for alt in itertools.product(*ranked): k = class="string">"".join(ALPHA[a] for a in alt) keys.add(k) if len(keys) >/= top_k: break class=class="string">"comment"># ensure baseline if len(keys) < top_k: k0 = class="string">"".join(ALPHA[s] for s in shifts) keys.add(k0) return list(keys)[:top_k] def suggest_vigenere_key_lengths(ct: str, max_len: int = class="number">16) ->/ list[int]: class=class="string">"comment"># combine kasiski factor votes + friedman closeness _, fac = kasiski_examination(ct, class="number">3, class="number">5, max_len) fr = friedman_by_keylen(ct, max_len) class=class="string">"comment"># score lens: high votes + being close to class="number">0.065 votes = {k:v for k,v in fac.items()} lens = {} for m, ic in fr: lens[m] = lens.get(m, class="number">0.0) + (max(class="number">0, class="number">0.065 - abs(class="number">0.065-ic)) * class="number">1000) for k,v in votes.items(): lens[k] = lens.get(k, class="number">0.0) + v * class="number">50.0 class=class="string">"comment"># rank ranked = sorted(lens.items(), key=lambda t: t[class="number">1], reverse=True) return [m for m,_ in ranked][:class="number">8] class=class="string">"comment"># ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- class=class="string">"comment"># Guessers registry class=class="string">"comment">#
